
clothes = {

	usage = game
	selection_behavior = weighted_random
	fallback = default_clothes

	no_clothes = {
        dna_modifiers = {
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = clothes
                template = no_clothes
                range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }
        }   
        outfit_tags = { no_clothes }
        weight = {
            base = 0
            modifier = {
                add = 1000
                should_be_fully_naked_portrait_trigger = yes
            }
            modifier = {
            	add = -1000
            	should_show_nudity = no
            }
        }
    }

    nightgown_western = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = western_sickness
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}
		outfit_tags = { no_clothes }
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 110
				should_show_nudity = no
				should_be_naked_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
            	add = -1000
            	should_show_nudity = yes
            }
            modifier = {
            	add = -50
				portrait_byzantine_clothing_trigger = no
				portrait_northern_clothing_trigger = no
				portrait_western_clothing_trigger = no
				portrait_french_clothing_trigger = no
				portrait_italian_clothing_trigger = no	
				portrait_gaelic_clothing_trigger = no			
				portrait_northern_slav_clothing_trigger = no	
				portrait_balto_finnic_clothing_trigger = no			
				portrait_iberia_clothing_trigger = no
			    portrait_hungarian_clothing_trigger = no	
				portrait_german_clothing_trigger = no	
				portrait_georgian_clothing_trigger = no	
				portrait_bulgarian_clothing_trigger = no
				portrait_armenian_clothing_trigger = no		
				portrait_south_slav_clothing_trigger = no					
            }
		}
	}

	nightgown_mena = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = mena_sickness
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}	
		outfit_tags = { no_clothes }
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 110
				should_show_nudity = no
				should_be_naked_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
            	add = -1000
            	should_show_nudity = yes
            }
            modifier = {
				add = 1100
				has_character_modifier = vow_of_poverty_modifier
			}
            modifier = {
            	add = -50
				portrait_mena_clothing_trigger = no
				portrait_indian_clothing_trigger = no
				portrait_steppe_clothing_trigger = no
				portrait_african_clothing_trigger = no
				#portrait_ghaznavid_clothing_trigger = no				
				portrait_seljuk_clothing_trigger = no
				portrait_dde_abbasid_clothing_trigger = no	
				portrait_iranian_clothing_trigger = no		
				portrait_south_indian_clothing_trigger = no		
				portrait_east_african_clothing_trigger = no		
				portrait_early_eastern_iranian_trigger = no	
				portrait_cuman_clothing_trigger = no	
				portrait_uyghur_clothing_trigger = no	
				portrait_iberia_muslim_clothing_trigger = no	
				portrait_maghreb_clothing_trigger = no	
			    portrait_Khazar_clothing_trigger = no	
			    portrait_kirghiz_clothing_trigger = no
				portrait_burmese_clothing_trigger = no		
			    portrait_tibetan_clothing_trigger = no					
            }
		}
	}

    poverty_robes_western = {
    	dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = western_sickness
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}
		weight = {
			base = 0
			# Boring clothes for characters with an active Vow of Poverty
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_character_modifier = vow_of_poverty_modifier
				# Should still wear armor when going to war
				NOT = { portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
            	add = -50
				portrait_byzantine_clothing_trigger = no
				portrait_northern_clothing_trigger = no
				portrait_western_clothing_trigger = no
				portrait_french_clothing_trigger = no
				portrait_italian_clothing_trigger = no	
				portrait_gaelic_clothing_trigger = no
				portrait_northern_slav_clothing_trigger = no	
				portrait_balto_finnic_clothing_trigger = no

				portrait_bulgarian_clothing_trigger = no
				portrait_armenian_clothing_trigger = no		
				portrait_south_slav_clothing_trigger = no					
            }
		}
    }

	default_clothes = {
        dna_modifiers = {
            accessory = {
                mode = add

	ruler_designer_clothes = {

				template = no_clothes
                range = { 0 1 }
            }
        }   
        weight = {
            base = 0
            modifier = {
            	add = 100			
            	exists = scope:ruler_designer
            }
        }
    }
		

## So that the Prophet Muhammad does not have a portrait ## 

	no_portrait = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add				
				gene = clothes
				template = no_clothes
				value = 0.5
			}
		}
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 2000
				this = character:33922
			}
		}
	}

## Small children ## 

	western_children = {

		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = western_children_commoner_clothes
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				age < 4
			}
		}
	}

## DDE HRE ##

	dde_hre_commoners = {

		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = dde_hre_commoner_clothes
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_dde_hre_clothing_trigger = yes
			}
			# ## Exclude characters with the has_scripted_clothes flag, mostly used for developer characters
   #          modifier = {
   #              factor = 0
   #              has_character_flag = has_scripted_clothes
   #          }
		}
	}
	
	dde_hre_low_nobles = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = dde_hre_low_nobility_clothes
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				OR = {
					AND = {
						highest_held_title_tier = tier_county
						NOR = {
							# has_dynasty = no
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 1
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						portrait_dde_hre_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_county
							NOR = {
								# has_dynasty = no
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_dde_hre_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}

	dde_hre_high_nobles = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = dde_hre_high_nobility_clothes
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_duchy
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 1
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						portrait_dde_hre_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_duchy
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_dde_hre_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}
	
	dde_hre_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = dde_hre_war_nobility_clothes
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 102		# slightly stronger than western war
				portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				portrait_dde_hre_clothing_trigger = yes
			 OR = {
				EPE_armor_era_late_medieval_trigger = yes	
				EPE_armor_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes						
				}				
			}
		}
	}

####Tribal Era Crusader
	tribal_era_western_crusades = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = tribal_era_western_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 110
				        EPE_armor_era_tribal_medieval_trigger = yes						
				OR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes					
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
					
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	byzantine_commoners = {

		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = byzantine_commoner_clothes
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_byzantine_clothing_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}

				add = 50
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 1
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						portrait_indian_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
								AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_indian_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}				

			}
		}
	}

					has_short_disease_trigger = yes #affliction that would plausibly leave them bedridden for treatment
					has_character_flag = use_sickness_clothes
				}
				OR = {
					portrait_mena_clothing_trigger = yes
					portrait_indian_clothing_trigger = yes
					portrait_steppe_clothing_trigger = yes
					portrait_african_clothing_trigger = yes
					portrait_iranian_clothing_trigger = yes	
					portrait_turkish_clothing_trigger = yes		
				    portrait_south_indian_clothing_trigger = yes	
				    #portrait_ghaznavid_clothing_trigger = yes	
				    portrait_seljuk_clothing_trigger = yes
				    portrait_dde_abbasid_clothing_trigger = yes		
				    portrait_east_african_clothing_trigger = yes
				    portrait_early_eastern_iranian_trigger = yes	
				    portrait_cuman_clothing_trigger = yes	
				    portrait_uyghur_clothing_trigger = yes	
				    portrait_iberia_muslim_clothing_trigger = yes	
			        portrait_Khazar_clothing_trigger = yes	
			        portrait_kirghiz_clothing_trigger = yes	
				    portrait_burmese_clothing_trigger = yes		
			        portrait_tibetan_clothing_trigger = yes						
				}
			}
		}
	}

## Steppe ##

	steppe_commoners = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = steppe_commoner_clothes
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_steppe_clothing_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}

	steppe_low_nobles = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = steppe_low_nobility_clothes
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				OR = {
					AND = {
						highest_held_title_tier = tier_county
						NOR = {
							# has_dynasty = no
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 1
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						portrait_steppe_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_county
							NOR = {
								# has_dynasty = no
								AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_steppe_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}

								has_government = republic_government

							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						portrait_steppe_clothing_trigger = yes

									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_african_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}

	sub_saharan_high_nobles = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = sub_saharan_high_nobility_clothes
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}		
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {

							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 1
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						portrait_african_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_african_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}

## Orthodox ##

	religious_orthodox_devoted_clothes = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = religious_orthodox_devoted_clothes
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}
		outfit_tags = { monk_outfit }
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 101
				is_male = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = devoted
					AND = {
						faith = {
							has_doctrine_parameter = vows_of_poverty_active
						}
						OR = {
							AND = {
								has_council_position = councillor_court_chaplain
								faith = {
									has_doctrine = doctrine_theocracy_lay_clergy
								}
							}
							is_theocratic_lessee = yes
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					faith = faith:orthodox
					faith = faith:armenian_apostolic
					faith = faith:coptic
					faith = faith:messalian
					faith = faith:bogomilist
					faith = faith:paulician
					faith = faith:nestorian
				}
			}
		}
	}

	    }

					has_character_flag = need_priest_outfit

					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				OR = {
					faith = faith:orthodox

					faith = faith:coptic

				NOT = {
					faith.religious_head = this
				}

		}

	outfit_tags = { monk_outfit }
	weight = {

		modifier = {
			add = 110
			OR = {
				has_character_flag = need_priest_outfit
				is_theocratic_lessee = yes
				AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				has_council_position = councillor_court_chaplain
			}
			OR = {
				religion = religion:hinduism_religion
			}
		}
	}
}

## Zoroastrian ##

religious_zoroastrian_high_clothes = {
	dna_modifiers = {
		accessory = {
			mode = add
			gene = clothes
			template = religious_zoroastrian_high_clothes
			range = { 0 1 }
		}
		morph = {
			mode = modify_multiply
			gene = gene_bs_bust
			value = 1.0
			template = bust_clothes
		}
		morph = {
			mode = modify_multiply
			gene = gene_bs_body_shape
			value = 1.0
			template = body_shape_average_clothed
		}
	}
	outfit_tags = { priest_outfit }
	weight = {
		base = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 100
			OR = {
				has_character_flag = need_priest_outfit
				is_theocratic_lessee = yes
				AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				has_council_position = councillor_court_chaplain
			}
			OR = {
				religion = religion:zoroastrianism_religion
				religion = religion:yazidi_religion
				religion = religion:zunism_religion
				faith = faith:mandeaism
				religion = religion:dualism_religion
			}
		}
	}

	religious_african_high_clothes = {
	    dna_modifiers = {
	        accessory = {
	            mode = add
	            gene = clothes
	            template = religious_african_high_clothes
	            range = { 0 1 }
	        }
	        morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average
			}
	    }
	    outfit_tags = { priest_outfit }
	    weight = {
	        base = 0
	        modifier = {
				add = 100
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = need_priest_outfit
					is_theocratic_lessee = yes
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
					has_council_position = councillor_court_chaplain
				}
				OR = {
					religion = religion:akom_religion

## Han chinese ##

	han_commoners = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = han_commoner_clothes
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_han_clothing_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}

	han_low_nobles = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = han_low_nobility_clothes
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				OR = {
					AND = {
						highest_held_title_tier = tier_county
						NOR = {
							# has_dynasty = no
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 1
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						portrait_han_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_county
							NOR = {
								# has_dynasty = no
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_han_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}

	han_high_nobles = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = han_high_nobility_clothes
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}		
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 1
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						portrait_han_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_han_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}

	han_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {

				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				portrait_han_clothing_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}

	central_african_commoners = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = central_african_low_nobility_clothes
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					has_government = theocracy_government
				}
				portrait_central_african_clothing_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}

									primary_title.tier > 1

	turkish_commoners = {

				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_turkish_clothing_trigger = yes								
			}
		}
	}

				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}

		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
			    OR = {
				any_parent = { highest_held_title_tier = tier_kingdom }
				any_parent = { highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire }				
						}				
				portrait_french_clothing_trigger = yes
				is_ruler = no					
				is_landed = no	
				is_married = no					
			}
		}

				value = 1.0

			}
		}

				add = 20

				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse

							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_french_clothing_trigger = yes
                NOT = { portrait_dde_hre_flavor_dlc_trigger = yes }

								highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_dde_abbasid_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	
				portrait_dde_abbasid_flavor_dlc_trigger = yes					
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}

	tahirid_dynasty_commoners = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = dde_abbasid_commoner_clothes
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					has_government = republic_government
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_tahirid_trigger = yes
				EPE_culture_era_early_medieval_trigger = yes				
			}
		}
	}

				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}			
		}		
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 1
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
				        portrait_early_eastern_iranian_trigger = yes	
						portrait_non_iranian_trigger = yes							
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
								AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
					    portrait_early_eastern_iranian_spouse_trigger = yes	
						portrait_non_iranian_trigger = yes		
						}
					}
				}				

			}
		}
	}

			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}

				portrait_iranian_clothing_trigger = yes	
				portrait_islamic_iranian_trigger = yes

###northern slav non dlc version
	northern_slav_non_dlc_commoners = {

		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = northern_commoner_clothes
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_northern_slav_clothing_trigger = yes
                NOT = { portrait_norse_flavor_dlc_trigger = yes } 						
			}
		}
	}

	cuman_early_commoners = {

			}

				value = 1.0

			}

						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_hungarian_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}

	Khazar_high_nobles = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = Khazar_high_nobility_clothes
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 1
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						portrait_Khazar_clothing_trigger = yes
						
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_Khazar_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}

####Tribal Era teutonic Crusader
	tribal_era_teutonic_crusades = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = tribal_era_western_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				value = 1.0
				template = bust_clothes
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 112
				        EPE_armor_era_tribal_medieval_trigger = yes		
				OR = {
					portrait_german_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
				    portrait_dde_hre_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes						
				}						
				OR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes					
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
					
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						portrait_german_clothing_trigger = yes						
						
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_german_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes						
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}

				add = 20

				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse

							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_burmese_clothing_trigger = yes
			}
		}

				add = 50
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 1
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						portrait_georgian_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
								AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_georgian_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}

	            range = { 0 1 }
	        }

				value = 1.0

			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply
				gene = gene_bs_body_shape
				value = 1.0
				template = body_shape_average_clothed
			}
	    }
	    outfit_tags = { priest_outfit bishop_outfit }
	    weight = {
	        base = 0
	        modifier = {
				add = 150
				EPE_culture_era_early_medieval_trigger = yes					
				portrait_northern_clothing_trigger = yes
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = need_priest_outfit
					is_theocratic_lessee = yes
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				religion = religion:christianity_religion
				NAND = {
					faith = faith:catholic
					faith.religious_head = this
				}
				NOT = {
					faith = faith:orthodox
				}
				# NOT = {
					# faith = {
						# has_doctrine_parameter = vows_of_poverty_active
					# }
				# }
			}
	    }
	}
